    `crates/runtime` depends on `crates/types` (via `g3rs-garde-config-checks-types`), but this crosses the boundary of the root workspace. Depending on internal crates couples you to another package's structure. Depend on the root workspace's facade crate instead.
  [Error] g3rs-arch/shared-flag-required crates/runtime/Cargo.toml non-child dependency requires shared flag
    `crates/runtime` depends on `crates/types` (via `g3rs-garde-config-checks-types`), but `crates/types` is not marked as shared. Dependencies on non-child crates are forbidden by default to prevent coupling. If this crate is genuinely a shared dependency (types, contracts, utilities), add `shared = true` under `[package.metadata.guardrail3]` in its Cargo.toml. Otherwise, depend on the parent facade instead.

    `crates/runtime` depends on `crates/types` (via `g3rs-garde-source-checks-types`), but this crosses the boundary of the root workspace. Depending on internal crates couples you to another package's structure. Depend on the root workspace's facade crate instead.
  [Error] g3rs-arch/shared-flag-required crates/runtime/Cargo.toml non-child dependency requires shared flag
    `crates/runtime` depends on `crates/types` (via `g3rs-garde-source-checks-types`), but `crates/types` is not marked as shared. Dependencies on non-child crates are forbidden by default to prevent coupling. If this crate is genuinely a shared dependency (types, contracts, utilities), add `shared = true` under `[package.metadata.guardrail3]` in its Cargo.toml. Otherwise, depend on the parent facade instead.

    `crates/runtime` depends on `crates/types` (via `g3rs-release-config-checks-types`), but `crates/types` is not marked as shared. Dependencies on non-child crates are forbidden by default to prevent coupling. If this crate is genuinely a shared dependency (types, contracts, utilities), add `shared = true` under `[package.metadata.guardrail3]` in its Cargo.toml.
